Acrophobia /ˌækrə'foʊbiə/ is a noun that means an extreme or irrational fear of heights. In Chinese, it can be translated as 高空恐惧症 (gāokōng kǒngjù zhèng).

Canny /'kæni/ is an adjective that means shrewd or clever. In Chinese, it can be translated as 精明的 (jīngmíng de).

Pedal /'pɛdəl/ can be used as a verb or a noun. As a verb, it means to operate or control with pedals. As a noun, it refers to a lever operated by the foot to control a device. In Chinese, it can be translated as 踩踏 (cǎità) as a verb, and 踏板 (tàbǎn) as a noun.

Please note that 'acrophobia' and 'pedal' are above a middle school level, while 'canny' is a high school level word.

1. sow [soʊ] - to plant seeds (播种)
2. invade [ɪnˈveɪd] - to enter a place or situation where you are not wanted or welcome (入侵)
3. improvise [ˈɪmprəˌvaɪz] - to invent or make something without preparation (临时凑合)

   - 未被感动的；冷漠的

2. Somatic /səˈmætɪk/ (adjective)
   - Relating to the body, especially as distinct from the mind
   - 身体的；肉体的

3. Fig /fɪɡ/ (noun)
   - A soft, pear-shaped fruit with many small seeds inside
   - 无花果

- 国际音标：/ˈæstərɪsk/
- 英文解释：a symbol (*) used to mark printed or written text, typically as a reference or to indicate the omission of letters or words.
- 中文解释：星号，用来标记印刷或书写的文本，通常作为参考或表示省略字母或单词的符号。

2. loutish
- 国际音标：/ˈlaʊtɪʃ/
- 英文解释：uncouth and aggressive in a boisterous manner.
- 中文解释：粗鲁的，粗野而咄咄逼人的。

3. crumble
- 国际音标：/ˈkrʌmbəl/
- 英文解释：break or fall apart into small fragments, especially over a period of time as part of a natural process.
- 中文解释：崩溃，破碎，特别是随着时间的推移而变成小碎片，作为自然过程的一部分。
